                (or (= -f on) (and (= -c off) (= -u off)))))
      (a!3 (and (= -t off)
                (= -S off)
                (or (= -f on) (and (= -u off) (= -c off)))))
      (a!5 (and (= -o off)
                (= -n off)
                (or (= -m on) (and (= --full-time off) (= -g off) (= -l off))))))
(let ((a!4 (or (and (= -m on) (or (= -U on) a!2))
               (and (= --full-time off)
                    (= -g off)
                    (= -l off)
                    (or (= -U on) a!3)))))
(let ((a!6 (or (and (= -X on) (or (= -x on) a!1))
               (and (= -x on) (or (= -U on) a!2))
               (and (= -n off) (= -o off) a!4)
               (and (= -v on) (or (= -x on) a!5)))))
  (and (= -F off)
       (= --file-type off)
       (= -R off)
       (= -p off)
       (= -Z off)
       (= -s off)
       (= --version off)
       (= --help off)
       a!6))))
